iQVW64.SYS

Description

iQVW64.SYS is a vulnerable driver and more information will be added as found.

  • UUID: 4dd3289c-522c-4fce-b48e-5370efc90fa1
  • Created: 2023-05-06
  • Author: Nasreddine Bencherchali
  • Acknowledgement: |

DownloadBlock

This download link contains the vulnerable driver!

Commands

sc.exe create iQVW64.sys binPath=C:\windows\temp\iQVW64.SYS type=kernel &amp;&amp; sc.exe start iQVW64.SYS
Use Case Privileges Operating System
Elevate privileges kernel Windows 10
